#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x2139 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x213A [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x30FB)
  2: 0x213D [0x46] CAMERA_CONTROL: Disable user control
  3: 0x213F [0x38] SET_CLIENT_EVENT_MODE(mode=19*)
```
